I know this doesn’t answer the question, but… How much (or little) do you have to know someone to consider that person a stranger? Let’s be honest here. Even when you are in a relationship, you are still getting to know each other. The stories on this thread involve (most at least) some initial screening by the perspective hookup partners: a drink, some conversation, etc. So you know someone for say, 3 hours. Are they still a stranger after 3 hours? You could easily date someone for 2 weeks and go on only 2 lunch dates. From your perspective, you’re dating. You have known each other for 2 weeks. But the truth is you have only spent about 2 hours together. And sure, there are lots of women who won’t sleep with a guy on the first date. But how many of you will on the second…or push it to the third date (if you can push it that far without the partner losing interest)? So you manage to spread the total hours you know that person over several weeks. Is that any different than if you had all the hours at once? I might concede that the extra time gives you an opportunity to think about your feelings, but you don’t really know the person any better than before. Have you ever exaggerated how long you have known your partner just to make it seem to your friends or family like you really know each other? Yeah, we’ve been dating for a few weeks…(actually 9 days…). I think in many ways social media makes it worse, because you gain that false sense of security of actually knowing someone when you may have exchanged about 500 characters worth of text without actually saying anything of value. Let’s just say it happens. I had a friend from college (it was West Point so we didn’t get out much). He married the girl he was dating right after graduation. A mutual friend added it up and calculated that they had been in each others physical presence for total of 22 hours. This is before we had text, Skype, e-mail, etc. In case you are wondering, they ended in divorce. Don’t get me wrong. I’m not being judgmental here. I have seen other cases where the relationship worked out when the partners knew each other for even less time than that. I think in the end it comes down to having the right connection with a person. You can get that connection in an instant or after a few years. So maybe the real question is…what makes someone a stranger (or not)?

Not exactly sex with a stranger but about as close as it gets.
